  * grade_story_105.txt (grade=6.8)
    The plot effectively uses the "jolt" action to drive narrative progression, creating moments of revelation that propel the story forward. The structure maintains coherence with a clear beginning (discovery), middle (confrontation), and resolution (transformation), impressive within the tight constraints. However, the causal relationships between some events remain murky - particularly how the scholar gained power over the witch's domain and why the garage ultimately collapsed. The narrative logic sacrifices clarity for symbolic resonance in several critical moments.

The initial mystery of the chest transitions smoothly into metaphysical cooking, but the mechanics of how recipes physically manifest remains underdeveloped.
